  ', Published on Sep 2, 2015', Harvest International School is a residential coeducational community affiliated to Cambridge international Examinations. Harvest Campus is situated in the lush greenbelt area of Punjab, approximately thirty kilometer from the center of the bustling city of Ludhiana. It is the home of our International School and our Tennis Academy, located within a kilometer of each other. We also have spacious playing fields, an aviary, an organic farm and an arboretum, where one can walk in the midst of lovely scenic surroundings. Harvest International School is a residential coeducational community affiliated to Cambridge international Examinations. We focus on holistic development, addressing three main areas of education:', Academic excellence validated by the international recognized gold-standard of Cambridge\u2019s Advanced Level qualifications.', The personal growth of all students so they have resilience, confidence and firm moral values in an ever-changing and often bewildering world.', The transferable skills and life skills that are so eagerly sought by employers and leaders. These skills include fluent English Communication, social and organizing skills, and lifelong learning.', Harvest Tennis academy, renowned as the best-appointed academy in the country, if not in Asia, has produced many high ranking national tournament champions. Fourteen flood-lit deco-turf and clay courts are supervised by our expatriate and domestic coaches and our high-performance tennis players have the services of quality hitting partners, fitness coaches, a physiotherapist, dietitian and medical staff.',   ',

  ', Published on Sep 2, 2015', Harvest International School is a residential coeducational community affiliated to Cambridge international Examinations. Harvest Campus is situated in the lush greenbelt area of Punjab, approximately thirty kilometer from the center of the bustling city of Ludhiana. It is the home of our International School and our Tennis Academy, located within a kilometer of each other. We also have spacious playing fields, an aviary, an organic farm and an arboretum, where one can walk in the midst of lovely scenic surroundings. Harvest International School is a residential coeducational community affiliated to Cambridge international Examinations. We focus on holistic development, addressing three main areas of education:', Academic excellence validated by the international recognized gold-standard of Cambridge\u2019s Advanced Level qualifications.', The personal growth of all students so they have resilience, confidence and firm moral values in an ever-changing and often bewildering world.', The transferable skills and life skills that are so eagerly sought by employers and leaders. These skills include fluent English Communication, social and organizing skills, and lifelong learning.', Harvest Tennis academy, renowned as the best-appointed academy in the country, if not in Asia, has produced many high ranking national tournament champions. Fourteen flood-lit deco-turf and clay courts are supervised by our expatriate and domestic coaches and our high-performance tennis players have the services of quality hitting partners, fitness coaches, a physiotherapist, dietitian and medical staff.',   ',
